1b1(1): #rgya gangs/ badra pra ba mar yul ra dzunam 'ong skad du/ 
1b2(1): ba spyan ras garigs dbang phyug gi rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal byang chub sems dpa' 'phags pa stan ras gzigs dbang phyug
1b3(1): thugs rje chen po dang ldan pa legs pas phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa'i dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das hi mam pa'i
1b4(1): tshal chen po can dan sdong po dang / myu gu rgyas pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi tshogs chen po dang / thabs gcig tu bzhugs te/ 'di lta ste/ 
1b5(1): tshe dang ldan pa 'od srung chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa ga la 'od srung dang / tshe dang ldan pa rangs pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa kun 'ga' de gzhon nu
1b6(1): dang / tshe dang ldan par 'gags pa dang / tshe dang ldan pa/ ri'i bu dang / tshe dang ldan pa 'o dal gyi bu chen po dang / tshe dang ldan pa
2a1(1): @#/ rab 'bor la sogs pa dge slong gi dge 'dun chen po stong nyis brgya lnga bcu dang / byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'di lta ste
2a2(1): pad+ma dkar po dang / nyi 'od dang / gzungs kyi dbang phyug rgyal po dang / pad+ma'i spyan dang / ye shes dbang phyug dang / pad+ma dbang phyug dang / 
2a3(1): po dang / rin chen snying po dang / ku tu bzang po dang / sgrib pa rnam sel dang / nam mkha'i snying po dang / byams pa dang / sa'i snying po
2a4(1): dang / 'jam dpal dang / 'jig rten dpal dang / phyag na da dang / blo gros mi zad pa dang / nam mkha'i mdzod dang / blo gros
2a5(1): rgya mtsho dang / mthu chen po thob pa dang / zla 'od dang / dra ba can gyi 'od dang / spobs pa brtsegs pa dang / mya ngan dang mun pa thams cad
2a6(1): sel ba blo gros la sogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po grangs med pa dang / gnan yang gtsor byams pa la gnas pa'i dge slong
2a7(1): mang po dang / dge slong mang po dang / dge bsnyen dang / dge bsnyen ma mang po dang / lha'i tshogs dang / klu'i tshogs dang / de bzhin du
2b1(1): gnod sbyin dang / dri dang / lha ma yin dang / nam mkha' lda nga/ ma'as cing / go phyechen po dang / thul bub dang / da
2b2(1): mi dang mi ma yin pa bye ba phrag drug dang / khro bo chen po rdo rje hUM dang / rdo rjegashin rje gzed dang / rdo rje gnan gyis mi thub pa dang / rdo rje rnamagrin dang / 
2b3(1): rdo rje bgegs mthar byed dang / rdo rje gtsug gtor dang / rdo rje gnod mdzes rgyal po la sogs pa bdun cu dang / spyan ma dang / mA ma ki dang / 
2b4(1): na bza' dkar mo dang / sgrol ma dang / 'od zer can dang / dbyangs can ma dang / ngag nal ma dang / khro ga nyer can dang / ri khrod ma dang / 
2b5(1): dug sel ma dang / nor rgyun ma dang / dkar mo dang / yid bzangs ma dang / rnam par rgyal ma dang / dpal 'phreng ma dang / sa 'dzin
2b6(1): bzang mo dang / rdo rje dbang phyug ma la sogs pa stong drug brgya dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// de'i tshe 'khor de dag thams cad kyis/ 
2b7(1): bcom ldan 'das bla ma la bkur sti dang / rim gro'i phyir mchod pa du mas mchod cing / bsngags dra mas bstod par byed do// de nas bcom ldan 'a
3a1(1): thub pa chen po thugs rje chen po yongs su 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// snyoms pa
3a2(1): thugs mthag tus chen po rnam pa drug cu g.yos shing ltas bcoM rgyad du byung to// de'i lus ton yong nas/ bdu'i rgyal po sgra sgrogs shin tu snyoms padang
3a3(1): ldan nas/ rang gi 'khor dri ma darang lcags so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis sgra sgrogs bya ba'i sems kyi rtog pazugs su chud/ spu'i gnas thams
3a4(1): de nas 'od gzer bye ba drag dum byung ngo // 'od gzer de dang sa g.yos pa de dag gis phyogs bcu'i sangs kyi zhing thams cad kyang gsal bar gyur to// 
3a5(1): de'i tshe sgra sgrogs snyoms pa dang bcas pas/ de'i 'khor thams cad kyis 'dzam bu'i gling du khams nad la sogs pas rnam par 'che ba de// thugs
3a6(1): kyis yongs su dgongs nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gdong bcu gcig pa/ drang srong
3a7(1): rig sngags 'chang bye ba phrag 'gye stong dang lhan cig/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar lhags naso/ nabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ g.yas phyogs
3b1(1): su bar ba byas nas/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod // de nas sangs rgyas kyi mthus lha'i tshogs kyinang nas/ lha'i burin po che pad+ma'i drabs brgyan pa zhes bya ba bzhengs
3b2(1): thal mo sbyar nas// byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug la 'di skad ces smras so// kye ma mgon po thugs rje can/ 
3b3(1): rig sngags 'chang ba'i tshogs dang bcas// che ba'i byin brlabs ldan pa rnams/ sgra sgrogs skems pa gnom pa dang // nyon mongs btsucad nas gcod pa dang
3b4(1): sems can rnams la phan pa dang // bdag la shin tu smon pa'i phyir// sku dang rjes su mthun pa yi// rig sngags sbyor khyad par can// snying po dam pa bshad du
3b5(1): gsol// de tshe 'khor tshogs thams cad kyis// mkha' phyogs me tog char gyis bkang // bcom ldan thub pa'i dbu la ni// rin chen me tog gdugs su gyur/ 
3b6(1): lha rnams gtsang bar sbyar ba yi// yon chab bdug spos mi dri ba shos// ci 'byor dang bstobs kyis bral// thub pas nam mkha'i mdzod du brlabs// lha la bum
3b7(1): du ma yis// ro lo mo sil snyan 'phan gdugs dang // bla bre rgyal mtshan lngab lnga ba dang // lnga ljin bza' du mas mchod// de nas mgon po spar ras gzigs/ ba
3b8(1): gzhon nu'i nal mnga' bas// bzhengs 'jum thal mo sbyar nas ni// ston pa la ni 'di skad gsol// sde sdigs bzhin gyi bsnams pa dang // mda' dang rtsal gyi dregs pa'i
4a1(1): steng 'di ni legs brtsams las byung min// shin tu log pa las kyang min// sngon du sangs rgyas gdong mdzes kyi// bstan pa la yang gi
4a2(1): btang ba'i// bsod nams grangs kyis byung ba yin// lag pa du mar byang 'phrul pa ni// zas dang snod spyad gos nor rgyan// bskal pa ban+de bcu'i mchod sbyin te// 
4a3(1): nas rtsal dang shugs kyang yin// mda' ni b+hing gi ri ti'o// byin rlabs sngon du byid mod kyang // grangs mngaso tshul khrims 'bral bas ni// srin po'i rigs su 'khrungs pa
4a4(1): dang 'khor bcas gzhan la gnod 'gyur yin// ngas ni ngang tshul rlang byung ba'i// lus kyis bde gshegs mchod sbyin dang // bsgrub brtson legs byas mtha' yas la
4a5(1): spyod pa zas la gnas skal grangs// gang+gA klung gi rdul dang mtshungs// de snyed 'bras bu de tsam ste// dang blo las can dzaji snyed la// phan gdags pa ni bya ba'i phyir/ 
4a6(1): cung zad bsdus nas bshad pa ste// legs par nyon la yid la zung // sngon che 'das dus bskal ba ni// gad+hA'i klung bcu'i snga rol gyi// cher 'das pa'i snga rol na// 
4a7(1): gshegs rjog ces sangs rgyas kyi mtshan// man+ta ra yi dri zhes bya/ 'jig rten ston pa byung ba'i tshe// bdag ni khyim bdag grags par 'gyur// thub pa de la rig sngags mnos
4a8(1): mthong ma thag tu bskal pa'i grangs// bzhi khri snyed kyi 'khor ba bstil// de rjes bskal pa bad+ma'i klung // bye ma snyed cig snga rol na// bde gshegs rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi mtshan
4b1(1): thogs rnyed pad+ma brgya'i spyan// gtsug gtor yon dan rab rgyas pa'i// 'od zer rgyal po zhes bya ba// 'jig rten par bzhugs pa'i che// bdag nyid drang srong bdag por gyur// rig
4b2(1): sdigs 'di mnos bsgrubs pa yis// phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas nal mthong zhing // skye med chos la bzod pa thob// de rjes 'das dus bskul ba ni// bye ba phrag brgya'i snga
4b3(1): na/ bde gsheg sa rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi mtshan// tshe dpag med ces 'jig rten du// ston pa byang bdag gis mnos// de tshe phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyis/ 
4b4(1): bdag la dbang bskur lung bstan mdzad// khyod kyis sngon du bskal pa'i grangs// brjod mi lang nas rig sngags phyir// yang dag stong phrag stong snyed kyang // dang ba'i
4b5(1): mchod sbyin chen por byas// bye ba phrag grangs bcu gcig du// phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dbang bskur blangs// de dang de'i rnam sbyin mchog/ sangs rgyas zhing khams rab 'byam
4b6(1): dra yang dang yang du 'byung bar 'gyur// phyis ni 'dren pa shAkya zhes// mi mjed 'jig rten khams 'khrungs che// mi yul las kyang khyad bor du// yi dgas gling du skyes pa 'ga'// stan ladang
4b7(1): 'dud 'phel ba'i phyir// mtshan mo mun nag sprin rum du// skad cig glog 'gyu ci lta bar// rig sngags 'chang ba gdong bcu gcig/ yan lag stong dang ldan pa la// spyan ni tshig stong sum cu pa'i/ mtshan
4b8(1): dang ldan pa'i sgra 'byang 'gyur// da tshe skal ldan la la zhig/ mtshan nas brjod cing skal mos// rig sngags zlas pa po gang zhig/ 'jig rten 'dod pa kun 'grub cing // phyi nas ye shes nyi shar 'gyur/ 
6a1(1): 'byung ba ltas mchod dang // nams kyang ngan 'gror mo 'gro dang // bde ba can nam de 'drar skye// rigs sngags 'di dang sangs rgyas kyi// ye shes snying po 'dzin pa
6a2(1): labyang chub sems dang sangs rgyas kyi// rnam par thar pa'i chos sgo thob// bskal pa du mar dge bsags dang // rig sngags 'di snyed 'gyur ba ste// dad ldan khrel yang nga rgya shes
6a3(1): blo bzang bcon ldan snying rje che// mdog dkar dang bzangs gsong por smra// sems 'jam lus ngag dal bar spyod// bla ma la gus brtul zhugs che// sred pa chung zhing sprin la dga'
6a4(1): sangs rgyas la gus sems bcas pas// nyin mtshan rgyun du rig sngags 'don// bcu pa ni 'am ni bco lnga dang // khyad par du ni ches brgyad la// gso slong skra'i mdun du blang / 
6a5(1): skyon med tsan dan dkar bsogs zhing // rigs bzang las byang sgra gzugs sam// yang na sa rdor ni chen sogs// bzang las bde bar gshegs gzugs bya// yang na ris su
6a6(1): bris kyang rung // skra cig blo lha tshogs kyi// dkyil 'khor rgyas par byas pa la// mngon sum bzhin du dmigs byas na// myur du mngon gsum mthong bar 'gyur// yon tan
6a7(1): kun gyis brgyan pa yi// bum pa chu dang bcas pa la// sngags brjod pas ni 'dod don kun// grub 'gyur the tshom mi bya'o// nad dang 'phrod pa'i sman rnams la// sngags bzlas
6a8(1): za ba 'am lus la byug/ bdug pa tsam yang gnod pa sel// srad bu'am ni gos dag dang // phyag rgyas gdags kyang de bzhin no// 'dod pa gang dang gang la yang // me yi
6b1(1): las kyis sbyar bar bya// gsang sngags 'ad badzini med 'das// bdag kya rjes su 'jug par bya// de da gsungs pa'i dmangag/ byang chub sems dpa'a'ajam dbyangs kyis
6b2(1): sngags kyi ngo bo nyid lani// tshad du brjod pa 'di brjod do// e ma rang bzhin med pa'i tshes// sna tshogs gzugs su snang ba la// brjod rtag bral ba'i skad cig ni// ni 'a
6b3(1): che ba nyid yin no// srid pa dngos po med pa la// dmigs par byed pa bsgom pa'o// dmigs pa mthar zug med mthongangon// de ni bsgom pa'i 'bras bu'o// kun tu bzang bas gsang
6b4(1): sngags kyi don la ched du 'di ltar brjod// em sku gsum tha dad par// lus ngag yid kyi don las byung // don cig pa yi rnal 'byor gyis// sku gcig du ni nges par gzung / 
6b5(1): gang la gang phan skyed pa la// 'ja' tshon bzhin du snang mod kyang // tshig gis brjod pa'i yul mde// ye shes skal dpe ba med// sgrib pa rnam se la las la ni// ched du brjod pa 'a
6b6(1): ltar brjod/ e ma dngos po za nyid// ma byung ma skyes ma 'gags pa// skye 'gag lta bu'i tshe 'bral ni// skra dang phyag rgya sngags su snang // yon tan chu yi rlabs bzhin du// skye ba'i ngo
6b7(1): la gsal bar byed// nan tan gyis ni de nyid kyang // rgyu ba med par khong du chud// byang chub sems dpa' sa snying gis// rgyu la ched du 'di brjod do// e ma rang bzhin rnam dag la/ 
6b8(1): thogs med blo yi mun pa'i dbyings// rnam rtog bag chags kyis bkrus nas// blo bur dkar nag las su snang // dkar po sangs rgyas chos dge 'dun// de la sgro btags byang chub
7a1(1): sems de las byung ba'i 'phrin las kyis// nyon mongs las kyi sgrib pa stong byed// mgon po byams pas sngags bsgrub kyis// lam la ched du 'di
7a2(1): ltar brjod/ e ma gdod nas grol zhi'i sems// chu ltar dang bar snang mod kyang // sna tshogs 'gro bo'i gzugs 'byung bas// mun pa thibs par rnam par bsgyur// de nyid sems
7a3(1): kyi snang ba'i phyir// 'bad rtsol med pa'i sems kyis dkrol// rtsol ba med sems kyi dri mas ni// dri ma med pa'i sems 'tshong 'gyur// nam mkha'i snying po'i sngags mi nga la// ched du 'di
7a4(1): ltar brjod par mdzad// e ma stong pa mtshan ma bral/ kha dog dbyibs bral chos nyid bdag/ dag pa'i sems tshan gsal byed pa// shes rab chen po'i yi ge man// mtshan dpe ye
7a5(1): shes bde ldan skra// gang gang don du de snad sku// snying rje chen po'i ring shugs kyis// 'byung 'gyur yi ge tra'i don// byang chub sems dpa' pad+mos ni// gnas la ched du 'di ltar
7a6(1): brjod/ e ma rgyu rkyen nam mkha' la// nyi zla dkar rgyun 'khor ba yos// gsal nas nyin mtshan bye brag brjod// nyon mongs ma rig sred len gyis// 'du byed srid pa'i ma
7a7(1): bskul te// rnam shes mi gzugs skye mched drug/ reg cher skye dga' shi sdug bsngal// gsal byed dag pa nyid kyis dag/ phyag na rdo rjes 'bras don la// ched du brjod pa
7a8(1): 'di brjod do// e ma rab cing rgya chog// sngags mthu blan med pa yi/ sangs rgyas su stegs kyis migs// shes pa nyid kyang rdzas med pa// shes bya rdzas supa la med/ 
7b1(1): shes rapa'ang yul gyi rnam par na// rtag pa'i gzung 'dzin gyis bsgos pa// debang nas na thal bar 'gyur// danas dag pa'is rtags// sras da ma tag ra byud cing // bsnyen pa sa
7b2(1): kyi glu yos ni// mgon bstan ras gzigs la bstod// oM bcom ldan 'das mgon pa thugs rje spun ras gzigs// zhal grangs mdag dbyings du matsor yang snang // snang dang brtsa
7b3(1): dang bcu gcig drug dang gcig/ byams pa'i rnal bzangs mnga' ba'i mgon la phyag 'tshal lo// sran mo'i'o// oM ba dgyes zhal mdog du ma tsar yang 'gyur// la la byams pa snying rje dga'
7b4(1): ba'i nal/ la la 'dod rmongs ser sna chen po'o zhal// khro sdang gtum chags lha ldan phyag 'tshal lo// mA ma ka'i'o// oM phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dbang bskur rdzogs pa'i zhal// gtan pa med
7b5(1): pa'i mchod sbyin rgyal po'i phyag/ mdzad pa grangs med gus pa'i phyag rgyar ldan// bden gnyis zhabs kyis gshegs la phyag 'tshal lo// na bza' dkar me'i'o// oM mdza da ba thugs rje'i dbying
7b6(1): la thug med kyang / rtsom pa rgya mtsho rgyun mo 'chad mdzad pas// zhing rnams rgya mtsho rnam par sbyong ba yo// mgon po spyan ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo// sgrol ma'i'o// maM tsam gtso
7b7(1): ldan 'od zer 'gyed pa ltar// 'jug dgongs mi mnga' kun rtog mun bral yang // bskal pa rgya mchod khyad par don gsal ba'i// mgon po spyan ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo// 
7b8(1): 'od gzer can bgyi'o// oM sems can gyud 'gags mya ngan 'das pa che// 'dod chags byung ma thag tu yal ba ste// nyon mongs rtsub brtsal na po tha' med// mgon po spyan ras gzig
8a1(1): / la phyag 'tshal lo// dbyangs can ma'i'o// oM nyon mongs bdag tu bzung nas 'khor bar ste// de la yang yang brtags na ngan 'gror skye// rang bzhin
8a2(1): med par shes nas grol bar 'gyur// mgon po spyan ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo// phag gdong ma'i'o// oM chos rnams dag par mthong nas mtho sa thong // gnyis 'dzin
8a3(1): rtog pa chad na mya ngan 'das// sgyu ma'i sems dang ldan na gzhan don 'byung // mgon po spun sa ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo// khro gnyer can ma'i'o// oM rang bzhin spyod la chags
8a4(1): pas sa bon ru la// gzhan tshul dman par brjod pas zhing sa tshig/ lus ngag gtsang sde tso ma las byang chub ring // mgon po swan ras gzigs la phag 'tshal lo// sa 'dzin ma'i
8a5(1): 'o oM bdag nyid lha mun pa'i dug gi brgyal ba la// bdag med phyogs bral ye shes bdud rtsi sman// pha rol byin bcu srid dang rtogs stsal mdzad// mgon po spyan ras gzigs
8a6(1): la phyag 'tshal lo// dug sel ma'i'o// oM rang tshul bzang ba spyod nga rgyal zhen pa med// gzhan spyod btang snyoms byos nas rang sems spong // sred med bzod ldan dang gis
8a7(1): dgon pa logs// mgon po spyan ras gzigs la phyag 'tsha lo lo// ri khrod ma'i'o// oM khrol ngo tsha shes shing gtong la dga'// dad dong thos ldan tshul khrims shes rab bzang
8a8(1): chog shes 'dod chung 'di dang gzhan du phyag/ mgon po sman ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo// nor rgyun ma'o'o// oM yi ge bri mchog sbyin nyan thos klog dang 'chang / kha ton 'dzin pam
8b1(1): bsgom tsun de la chu'o// khrus sogs nyung dkar gtsang yon bsal// mgon pa sgron ras gzigs la phyog 'tshal lo// dkar mtha'//  rang sems rdul zhi yug dag bag yad spod/ 
8b2(1): 'jig rten 'das mchod dam pa 'dzin// thos bsam sgom brtson de ni dgra las rgal// mgon pa sprin ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo// rnam par rgyal ma'i hU~M'o// oM thaM dang kyos 'tshongs dbu
8b3(1): med grol ba'i rmyi// thabs dang shes rab bde chen byang chub lam// rnam thar ya shes mtha' yas dpal ster ba// mgon pa spyan ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo// dpal 'brang ma'i glan/ 
8b4(1): oM bsam pa bzang po gser gis gnil// byang chub phyogs chos dpag zas ma shing chen 'khrungs// ye shes thugs rje nu nan mdzad pa yi// mgon mo sran ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal la
8b5(1): yid bzangs ma'i'o// sgra sgrogs 'khor bcas 'dar 'gyur te// rlung gis btab pa'i rtswa dang mtshungs// thal mor spyi bor skur nas su// tshad du brjod pos 'di gsol to// oM mgon
8b6(1): mgon po rang bzhin 'byung bcom ldan 'das// gtso bor rab tu che ba'i lha// bsod nams du mas bskyed pa'i sku// ye shes mtha' yas thugs mnga' ba// blo ldan srid mthar mdzad pa pa
8b7(1): tshul ldan tshul khrims las spyod mdzad// gtsang ldan bram ze tshangs pa che// mdzad brjod mkha' mnyam spod phyag 'tshal// de nas bcom ldan thub pa ches// 'khor la legs se leg
8b8(1): se nas oM a ga thar bcas/ yang yang brjed ngas byin gyis brlabs// lcags kyu can gyi'i nas// grwa phyogs 'bum phrag 'dzin pa ltar// dge slong kun srad de
9a1(1): bos ni/ byang chub rin chen gling 'jog mdzad// / 'phags pa sran ras gzigs dbang phyug gi rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po pad+mo dra pa zhes bya ba las/ 
9a2(1): gleng gzhi'i le'u ste dang pa'o// de nas bcom ldan thub pa che// mgon po yang dag rdzogs sangs rgyas// sna tshogs snang ba zhes bya ba'i// ting nge 'dzin la snyoms
9a3(1): zhugs nas/ yan lag cha shas thams cad las// 'od zer sna lnga bye ba phrag/ drug bcu drug bcu'i mtha' gzhal ba// grangs med dag ni bkye bar mdzad// zhing rnams grangs med bdun gyi
9a4(1): mtha' phyogs bcu ma lus thams cad du// 'od kyis gang nas 'od de las// snyan pa'i tshigs bcad 'di snang ngo // sangs rgyas dang ni chos la brnyas pa spang // le lo tshe dang spod pa
9a5(1): pa mchog 'dzin spang // 'gyod dang chos la ma nges 'byed pa spang // nga rgyal tshe dang 'dad chags spyod pa yang // 'gro rnams med na byang chub lam med de// 'grol brtan nas byang chub che thatha
9a6(1): 'gyur/ byang chub che lam thugs rje chen po ste// 'gro rnams med na gang skye bar 'gyur// de skad grags pa'i de ma theg/ phyogs bcu'i zhing bzhugs sangs rgyas sras// brjod kyis
9a7(1): mi ling gtso bo mchog/ spyan ras gzigs dbang grangs med gtso// thams can 'khor dang bcas pa rnams// mi mjed zhing 'dir lhags par 'gyur// 'di nas shar phyogs zhing rnams ni
9a8(1): grangs med bdun gyi mtha' nyid nas// zhing khams seng ge 'brangs par ni// sangs rgyas seng ge rol pa yi// drung du byang chub sems dpa'i gtso// spyan ras gzigs dbang seng ge sgra/ 
9b1(1): mdog dkar shel gyi sku 'dab// byang chub sems mchag bu ba zag/ bcu nga cun cig mkha' ma gzhags/ klag 'gyur ba zhin du zhing 'dir byed// bcom ldan mnan pa thub pa la// byag

340a4(1): lagus pas dang / bla mar bgyis pa lags/ mchod pa dang / brjod pa bgyis pa lags so// de ska bas na dang pa'i rjes su 'brang bas byams pa bsgoms padang / sring rje ba cu
340a5(1): pas dngos grub chen po thob par 'gyur ro// ci sted gyi ba 'di las mang bar mi baching ba'i sems can de la bdag gis nag par rgyun ze 'chad par dran par dang / bdag 'dod pa tsam gyis
340a6(1): rang gi gzugs shin tu yongs su ngas pa'i rang gi ngo bos bdag mdun na mchis par rab gyi nyid yid la re ba thams ca dang / mchog yongs su rdzobs par brgya'o// 'aste/ bdag ni sgrar dam
340a7(1): bcas pa lag na nu bci ni/ bdag gis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag la bsdus pa lags pa/ lags sa// rig sngags kyi gangs pa/ rnam gyur pa san mo babyi
340a8(1): dam bcas gtsun du smra bar mo brtsi'i/ rig sngags 'chang gise nag tugaca na gyi na ga cu 'dram pa dang nag sa byams pa dang / sring du sgom pa yid la mabyed na/ des bdag gis nas
